<br><font size="+2"><b><a name="ipa"></a>ipa</b> </font>
<font size="+2">to eat (a certain thing)</font>
&nbsp;<font color="#800080" size="+1">-LI/3</font>
&nbsp;(<i>ispa, ilpa, haspa</i>)
&nbsp; [/(i)pa]
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Chaspaahi?
 <i>Are you going to eat me?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Chilpaaho.
 <i>We're going to eat you.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Chachimalostiiyok chaispahchálpìiso?
 <i>Do you like me so much you want to eat me? (Rabbit says to a dog).</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Eh, sobàylilo; ipalihchoolikha.
 <i>Yes, I know about it; I used to eat it a lot.</i> <font size="0">(NHN)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Nákson oɬachíik itaayíipok atòkla itaayíipòosit oíipat stittanowwahchoolo.
 <i>When they got somewhere they ate it on the ground and ate seconds and took it with them.</i> <font size="0">(NHN)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>

&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Istankanoomòolo.

&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Ya holikfaya ilhíicha stankáanobi.

<br><font size="+2"><b><a name="iyyoobàali"></a>iyyoobàali</b> </font>
<font size="+2">back part of the heel below the Achilles tendon </font>
&nbsp; [/iyyi /obàali]
 [<i>lengthening of initial /o/ for some speakers, found in other compounds</i>]
 <i>Var: iyyobàali</i>
&nbsp;<font size="0">(VC)</font>
<br><font size="+2"><b><a name="iyyowwa"></a>iyyowwa</b> </font>
<font size="+2">to call to, hail (someone); to invite, include in a group, welcome</font>
&nbsp;<font color="#800080" size="+1">-LI/AM-</font>
&nbsp;(<i>iyyochiwwa, iyyoliwwa, iyyohachiwwa</i>)
&nbsp; [im- /yowwa]
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Ayyówwàasaⁿ?
 <i>Was somebody calling me?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Iyyówwàasaⁿ?
 <i>Was he calling him?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>`Chahalkìi' mankat iyyowwatoha.
 <i>He called out `my wife' to her.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
